      <div class="post-5652 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-kungphoo tag-advertise-my-business-online tag-advertising tag-attract-people tag-chains-off-marketing tag-classifed-advertising tag-deals tag-definite-purpose tag-dojo-marketing tag-dojomarketing tag-free-advertising tag-free-advertising-websites tag-global-advertising tag-internet-marketing tag-kungphoo-2 tag-kungphoo-marketplace tag-kungphoo-com tag-local-advertising tag-local-business tag-marketing tag-marketplace tag-online-advertising tag-online-marketing tag-passion tag-phoo tag-promote tag-promote-my-business tag-promoting-your-business tag-purpose tag-sell-online tag-sell-online-free tag-seo tag-small-business tag-small-business-advertising tag-small-business-marketing tag-small-business-marketplace tag-small-business-struggle tag-social tag-social-marketing tag-social-marketplace tag-social-marketplace-for-small-business tag-step-into-the-dojo tag-success tag-support-local-business" id="post-5652">
       <div class="entry-meta-group clearfix2">
        <div class="grid_2 alpha">
         <span class="entry-date">
          <a href="http://www.kungphoo.com/blog/definite-purpose/" rel="bookmark" title="June 18, 2014 6:17 am">
           <span class="entry-date-day">
            18
           </span>
           <span class="entry-date-month-year">
            Jun 2014
           </span>
          </a>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div class="grid_8 omega">
         <h1 class="entry-title entry-title-single">
          Definite Purpose
         </h1>
         <div class="entry-meta">
          <span class="entry-author author vcard">
           <a href="http://www.kungphoo.com/blog/author/sensei/" rel="author" title="by Sensei">
            Sensei
           </a>
          </span>
          <span class="entry-meta-sep">
           
          </span>
          <span class="comments-link">
           <a href="http://www.kungphoo.com/blog/definite-purpose/#comments">
            166 Comments
           </a>
          </span>
         </div>
         <!-- .entry-meta -->
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="entry-content clearfix2">
        <p style="text-align: center;">
         <a href="http://www.kungphoo.com/blog/definite-purpose/">
          <img alt="Purpose, passion, success, attract people, definite purpose" class="wp-image-5655 aligncenter" height="310" src="http://www.kungphoo.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2014/06/got-purpose.jpg" width="400"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         Success is not something you become. Success is not something you pursue. Success is something you attract by the person you become. Success is something you attract by becoming an attractive person.
        </p>
        <p>
         The most important quality to attract success is a
         <a href="http://www.kungphoo.com" target="_blank">
          Definite Purpose
         </a>
         . You must know what you want. Definite means clearly stated or decided; not vague or doubtful: certain or sure about something.
        </p>
        <p>
         Millions of people go through life not knowing what it is they want. All people have a purpose, but few have a Definite Purpose. Nothing is impossible to the person who knows what it is he/she wants and makes up his/her mind to acquire it.
        </p>
        <p>
         Opportunity, capital, co-operation from others and all other essentials for success gravitate to the person who knows what they want. Nothing is impossible to the person with a Definite Purpose. Just like prayer, definite purpose based on faith always works.
        </p>
        <p>
         Singleness of purpose is one of the chief essentials for success in life, no matter what may be ones aim.  John D. Rockefeller, Jr.  See more at:
         <a href="http://www.kungphoo.com/circles/view/funtasticliving" target="_blank">
          http://www.kungphoo.com/circles/view/funtasticliving
         </a>
        </p>
        <div class="wp-caption alignnone" id="attachment_3319" style="width: 160px">
         <a href="http://www.kungphoo.com/blog/definite-purpose/">
          <img alt="Purpose, passion, success, attract people, definite purpose" class="size-thumbnail wp-image-3319 " height="150" src="http://www.kungphoo.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2013/12/kungphoo-sword-150x150.png" width="150"/>
         </a>
         <p class="wp-caption-text">
          <b>
           Voice of Small Business
          </b>
         </p>
        </div>
        <p>
         (
         <a href="http://www.kungphoo.com" target="_blank">
          http://www.kungphoo.com
         </a>
         ) is an easy to use, dynamic social marketing and commerce platform. You can buy, sell, promote or search for anything collectively with like-minded individuals by creating purpose-based circles that people can join to talk about or take advantage of. Listings are promoted within the kungphoo marketplace, Social Media and across the web.
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>

           </p>

   <script charset="utf-8" type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function(){
    $("a[rel^='prettyPhoto']").prettyPhoto();

    $("#gallery img").click(function(){
        $('#main-img').attr('src',$(this).attr('src').replace('thumb/', ''));

         var p_image = $('#main-img').attr('src');
         $("a.print-image").attr("data-print-src",p_image);
         $("a#main-photo").attr("href",p_image);

    });
    // Image preload
    var imgSwap = [];
     $("#gallery img").each(function(){
        imgUrl = this.src.replace('thumb/', '');
        imgSwap.push(imgUrl);
    });
    $(imgSwap).preload();
});
$.fn.preload = function() {
    this.each(function(){
        $('&lt;img/&gt;')[0].src = this;
    });

  }
   </script>
